style="width: 39px;">Aquaconsious</span></strong></h1>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;Large-scale AI Data Centers can take millions of gallons daily for cooling servers and generating electricity, while queries presented by users to AI chats take only a fraction of this.&nbsp;<em>This doesn&rsquo;t mean that queries are innocent, as those small amounts of water add up fast</em>.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;Did you know that&nbsp;<strong>14.33 million liters of water</strong>&nbsp;are used by Gemini Flass 2.5 alone each day? This is spread across the platforms 40 million daily users. This is enough water to fill about 130 swimming pools.&nbsp;</span></p>

<h2><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;"><strong>The problem: overuse</strong></span></h2>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;People ask AI for everything, from basic math and facts to writing emails. Each unnecessary AI query wastes water that could meet someone&apos;s daily drinking needs.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">When not to use AI:</span></p>

<table>

<tbody>

<tr>

<td>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Use Google for:</span></p>

<ul>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Basic facts</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Weather forecasts</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Store hours</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Contact information</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Definitions</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Searching for recipes or locations</li>

</ul>

</td>

<td>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Use a Calculator For:</span></p>

<ul>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Math problems</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Budget calculations</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Calculating tips</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Unit conversion</li>

</ul>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p>

</td>

</tr>

</tbody>

</table>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Before asking AI, be sure to ask, &ldquo;Do I actually need AI for this, or could I get this information somewhere else?&rdquo;</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">When you feel you need to use AI, be sure to:</span></p>

<ul>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Combine multiple questions into one prompt</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Be specific about what you need</li>

<li style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Save responses for later to avoid asking again&nbsp;</li>

</ul>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Your digital choices have real-world consequences. Every unnecessary AI question wastes water someone else needs.&nbsp;</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">Make it count!</span></p>

<p><span style="font-family: Verdana, Geneva, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></p>
